Born into a vacuum of poverty, Gibbs is an uncut distillation of his surroundings.<br /><br />Freddie&rsquo;s keen survivalist mentality and work ethic won him a scholarship to Ball State University for football, but he was dismissed over questionable allegations. Gibbs was cast back into the sink-or-swim realities of his upbringing, and he resorted to pimping and manufacturing freebase to keep the lights on. A humble critic, Freddie never meant to be a part of the problem, and explored means of supporting himself without partaking in the cyclical plague of drugs and prostitution. A gifted writer who stood out amongst his peers with his reserved wit and command of language, Freddie began to rap about the things he saw.<br /><br />As word of his skills spread to the coasts, he aligned himself with notable producers like The Alchemist, Red Spyda, Just Blaze, and Buckwild to create a discography that illustrates his experiences as a struggling denizen of a blighted community. In 2010, XXL Magazine caught wind of Freddie&rsquo;s unique approach and nominated Gibbs to their Freshman Top 10. Subsequently, Freddie Gibbs&rsquo; previous mixtapes, which capture the forsaken instrumental aesthetic of 90&rsquo;s boom-bap and juxtapose it with his distinctly Midwestern double-time flow, began to garner widespread critical acclaim and industry attention.<br /><br />The rapper also endeavored to expand his musical horizons by teaming up with UK dubsteb producer Joker on a remix of the track &ldquo;The Vision&rdquo; and with New York indie-noise-pop duo Cults on a reworking of their track &ldquo;Bad Things.&rdquo; His willingness to both function in the world of gangster rap and to step Doch vor allem steht er da als Brckenbauer,  zwischen sonst gnzlich anderen Hip Hop-Approaches.  Zwischen Gangsta Rap und dem sophisticated & freaked out  Stone Thrower-Stuff, wie er 2014 auf seinem grandiosen Kolaboalbum Piata mit Beat Mastermind Madlib bewies.
